## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics (ODE growth models)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt is an instantaneous population growth rate driven by current population size P and possibly explicit time forcing t (environmental variability, interventions). This aligns with classical ecological ODE models where density dependence, carrying capacity, Allee effects, and time-varying rates determine dP_dt(P,t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Malthusian (exponential) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent per-capita growth)
- Linear birth‚Äìdeath with immigration: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (net proportional growth plus constant influx/outflux)
- Logistic ODE (quadratic density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (self-limitation with carrying capacity proportional to 1/c1)
- Gompertz growth (logarithmic density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (per-capita growth decreases with log of size)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P) ** c2) (flexible strength/shape of density dependence)
- Richards-type generalized logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P) ** c2) * ((c3 * P) ** c4) (extra shape control for early/late growth regimes)
- Strong Allee effect (bistability): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 * P - 1) (growth negative below an Allee threshold and near crowding)
- Weak Allee effect modifier: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 - exp(-c2 * P)) (small-P suppression that vanishes at larger P)
- Density-dependent mortality (crowding loss): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P ** 2 - c2 * P ** 3 (higher-order crowding/competition effects)
- Proportional harvesting/effort: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (removal proportional to population size)
- Constant-yield harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (fixed removal; can create extinction thresholds)
- Seasonally forced growth rate: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) * P * (1 - c4 * P) (periodic environment acting on per-capita growth)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P / (c1 + c2 * exp(-c3 * t))) (approaching/relaxing habitat capacity over time)
- Pulse/step intervention approximation: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * tanh(c2 * (t - c3))) * P * (1 - c4 * P) (smooth transition in conditions at time c3)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ‚Üí Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ‚Üí Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ‚Üí Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ‚Üí Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ‚Üí Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If (dP_dt / P) is approximately constant across P, expect dP_dt ‚àù P (density-independent exponential regime).
- If dP_dt crosses zero at P=0 and at a positive P*, and is positive between them, expect a quadratic factor like P*(1 - c*P) (single carrying-capacity equilibrium).
- If dP_dt is negative at small P but positive at intermediate P, then negative again at large P, expect an Allee-type cubic structure with two positive equilibria (threshold + carrying capacity).
- If per-capita growth (dP_dt / P) declines roughly linearly with log(P), expect a Gompertz term P*log(c/P).
- If the location of the nonzero equilibrium shifts systematically with t, model time-varying parameters (e.g., carrying capacity c1 + c2*exp(-c3*t) or growth c0 + c1*sin(c2*t)).
- If growth is reduced by a nearly constant amount regardless of P (parallel downward shift in dP_dt vs P), include a constant harvest term (-c).
- If growth reduction scales with P (stronger reduction for larger populations), include proportional removal (-c*P) rather than a constant offset.
- If dP_dt vs P shows asymmetric rise/fall (slow start then rapid approach, or vice versa), use a shape parameter via (c*P)**c2 (theta-logistic/Richards-style curvature control).

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG12)
============================================================
GT: c0*P*sin(c1*t) + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed):
\[
0.8770002846\,P\sin(0.5671736066\,t)\;+\;0.7013915187(1-P/65.7541311409)P
\]
Expand the polynomial part:
\[
0.7013915187P - \frac{0.7013915187}{65.7541311409}P^2
\]
So GT is exactly of the form
\[
(\text{const})\,P\sin((\text{const})t)\;+\;(\text{const})P\;+\;(\text{const})P^2
\]
with **no** constant-only term, and **no** \(t\)-only terms like \(1/t\), \(1/(a t+b)\), \(t\), logs, exps, powers of \(P\) other than 1 and 2, etc. Therefore any candidate can match only if all extra non-GT functional forms can be set to zero, and the remaining terms can be tuned to the exact coefficients/frequency/phase.

Let
- \(A=0.8770002846\)
- \(\omega=0.5671736066\)
- \(B=0.7013915187\)
- \(C=-0.7013915187/65.7541311409\) (the \(P^2\) coefficient)

Also note: GT sine has **no phase shift**; but a candidate \( \sin(c_2 t + c_3)\) can match \( \sin(\omega t)\) by setting \(c_3=0\) (or any \(2\pi k\)) and \(c_2=\omega\).

---

### 1.
\(P^2c_0 + Pc_1\sin(c_2 t+c_3)+Pc_4+c_5+c_6/t+1/(c_7 t+c_8)\).  
To match GT, must remove \(c_5\), \(c_6/t\), and \(1/(c_7 t+c_8)\). The last term cannot be made identically 0 by any finite constants (it‚Äôs always a nonzero rational function). So cannot match.

### 2.
Has \(c_5 t/(c_6 t+c_7)+c_8/(c_6 t+c_7)\) which is a nontrivial rational-in-\(t\) term unless both numerators are 0. Setting \(c_5=c_8=0\) removes them. Then remaining \(P^2c_0 + Pc_1\sin(c_2 t+c_3)+Pc_4\) can match GT by choosing \(c_0=C\), \(c_1=A\), \(c_2=\omega\), \(c_3=0\), \(c_4=B\). **Matches.**

### 3.
Contains fixed \(+P^2\) and log term, plus \(c_6 t\), \(c_7/t\), constant \(c_8\). The \(+P^2\) cannot be removed (coefficient 1). GT‚Äôs \(P^2\) coefficient is \(C\neq 1\). No way to cancel with other terms (no other pure \(P^2\) term except \(P^2c_0\), which would just shift coefficient to \(c_0+1\), still could equal \(C\) by setting \(c_0=C-1\). But the log term \(c_4\log(Pc_5+1)\) must be removed: set \(c_4=0\). Also must remove \(c_6 t\) and \(c_7/t\): set \(c_6=c_7=0\). Then expression becomes \(P^2(c_0+1)+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)+c_8\). GT has no constant term, so set \(c_8=0\). Then can match with \(c_0=C-1\), \(c_1=A\), \(c_2=\omega\), \(c_3=0\). **Matches.**

### 4.
Same as 3 but with \(c_6/t+c_7/t\) (both removable by setting \(c_6=c_7=0\)), log removable by \(c_4=0\), constant removable by \(c_8=0\). Leaves \(P^2(c_0+1)+P c_1\sin(\cdot)\). But GT also has a linear \(+BP\) term; there is no \(Pc_4\) term here. So cannot match.

### 5.
Has \(c_5 t/(c_6 t+c_7)\) removable by \(c_5=0\), but also \(c_8/(c_7+t)\) which can be removed by \(c_8=0\). Then reduces to \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)+Pc_4\) and can match as in #2. **Matches.**

### 6.
Has log and \(1/t\) terms; set \(c_4=0\), \(c_6=c_7=0\), \(c_8=0\). Left with \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)\). Missing linear \(BP\). No match.

### 7.
Has \(c_5/t\) removable by \(c_5=0\), and \(c_6 t/(c_7 t+c_8)\) removable by \(c_6=0\). Then reduces to \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)+Pc_4\). Can match. **Matches.**

### 8.
Contains fixed \(+P^2\) (adjustable via \(c_0\) as in #3), but also \(P c_4\log(Pc_5+1)\) which must be removed by \(c_4=0\). Also has \(c_6/t+c_7/t+c_8\) removable by setting \(c_6=c_7=c_8=0\). Then left with \(P^2(c_0+1)+P c_1\sin(\cdot)\). Missing \(BP\). No match.

### 9.
Has \(P\) fixed (coefficient 1) plus \(P^{c_4}c_5\) and \(1/t\) terms. You can set \(c_6=c_7=c_8=0\). You can set \(c_5=0\) to remove \(P^{c_4}\) term. Then you have \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)+P\). But GT‚Äôs linear coefficient is \(B\neq 1\). No other linear \(P\) term to adjust it. No match.

### 10.
Has \(P c_4\log(Pc_5+1)\) removable by \(c_4=0\), and \(1/t\) terms removable by \(c_6=c_7=0\), constant by \(c_8=0\). Left with \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)\). Missing \(BP\). No match.

### 11.
Has \(P\) fixed, plus \(c_7 t\) and \(c_8/P^5\) etc. Even if set \(c_5=c_6=c_7=c_8=0\) and \(c_4=0\), still stuck with \(+P\) coefficient 1. GT needs \(B\neq 1\). No match.

### 12.
Same issue as 11: fixed \(+P\). No match.

### 13.
Has \(P^{c_4}c_5\) removable by \(c_5=0\), \(1/t\) terms removable by \(c_6=c_7=0\), constant by \(c_8=0\). Left with \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)\). Missing \(BP\). No match.

### 14.
Like 13 but with fixed \(+P^2\) (adjustable via \(c_0\)), still missing \(BP\). No match.

### 15.
Has \(c_6/t\) removable by \(c_6=0\), but also \(1/(c_8+t)\) which cannot be made identically 0 unless its coefficient were 0 (there is none). So cannot match.

### 16.
Has fixed \(+P\) coefficient 1; cannot adjust to \(B\neq 1\). No match.

### 17.
Contains \(P c_1(c_2+t)^{c_3}\) and \(\sin(Pc_5+c_6)\cos(c_7 t)\) etc; cannot reduce to a pure \(P\sin(\omega t)\) plus polynomial in \(P\) without leftover \(t\)-dependence or \(P\)-inside-sine dependence. No match.

### 18.
Has \(P c_4\log(1+c_5/P)\) removable by \(c_4=0\), \(1/t\) terms removable by \(c_6=c_7=0\), constant by \(c_8=0\). Left with \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)\). Missing \(BP\). No match.

### 19.
No \(P^2\) term at all; GT has nonzero \(P^2\) coefficient \(C\neq 0\). No match.

### 20.
No \(P^2\) term; rational \(P c_4/(P+c_5)\) cannot become a polynomial \(aP+bP^2\) for all \(P\). No match.

### 21.
No \(P^2\) term. No match.

### 22.
Has \(\text{Abs}(P)\) term; cannot equal a polynomial in \(P\) for all real \(P\) unless coefficient is 0, but even then remaining terms are \(P\) times a power in \(t\) etc and no \(P^2\) term. No match.

### 23.
No \(P^2\) term. No match.

### 24.
Has \(+\text{Abs}(P)\) with fixed coefficient 1 (not removable). No match.

### 25.
Has \(P c_5 e^{c_6 t}\) which can be removed by \(c_5=0\); has \(c_8/t\) removable by \(c_8=0\); constant \(c_7\) removable by \(c_7=0\). Then left with \(P^2c_0+P^2c_1+P c_2\sin(c_3 t+c_4)\). Missing linear \(BP\). No match.

### 26.
No \(P^2\) term. No match.

### 27.
No \(P^2\) term. No match.

### 28.
No \(P^2\) term. No match.

### 29.
Has \(1/(c_7 t+c_8)\) with no coefficient; cannot be removed. No match.

### 30.
Has \(c_4 t^{c_5}\) and \(1/t\) terms; can remove by setting \(c_4=0\), \(c_6=c_7=0\), \(c_8=0\). Leaves \(P^2c_0+Pc_1\sin(\cdot)\). Missing \(BP\). No match.

### 31.
Same as 30 but with fixed \(+P^2\); still missing \(BP\). No match.

### 32.
Has \(c_4/t\) removable by \(c_4=0\), constant \(c_5\) removable by \(c_5=0\), but has \(1/(c_6+t)\) not removable. No match.

### 33.
Has fixed \(+P^2\) and fixed \(+P^{-5}\) (since \(P**(-5)\) has coefficient 1), cannot remove \(P^{-5}\). No match.

### 34.

### 35.
Has \(c_4 e^{P c_5}\) removable by \(c_4=0\), \(1/t\) terms removable by \(c_6=c_7=0\), constant by \(c_8=0\). Left with \(P^2(c_0+1)+P c_1\sin(\cdot)\). Missing \(BP\). No match.

### 36.
